  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_5d06aaa2-dde5-469f-930e-6e0518d36c00'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText4262131219958394817" style="display:none">Since the moment of her defection from the PsyNet and into the SnowDancer wolf pack, Sienna Lauren has had one weakness. Hawke. Alpha and dangerous, he compels her to madness.<br /><br />Hawke is used to walking alone, having lost the woman who would’ve been his mate long ago. But Sienna fascinates the primal heart of him, even as he tells himself she is far too young to handle the wild fury of the wolf.<br /><br />Then Sienna changes the rules and suddenly, there is no more distance, only the most intimate of battles between two people who were never meant to meet. Yet as they strip away each other’s secrets in a storm of raw emotion, they must also ready themselves for a far more vicious fight…<br /><br />A deadly enemy is out to destroy SnowDancer, striking at everything they hold dear, but it is Sienna’s darkest secret that may yet savage the pack that is her home…and the alpha who is its heartbeat…</span>

          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_11006334').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});

            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/119438412?book_show_action=true">Aug 31, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dina" href="/user/show/1918270-dina">Dina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780575105676" href="/book/show/10828497-kiss-of-snow">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1918270-dina?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer119438412" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10734437748104996394">First off, let me say that I'm completely biased when it comes to Hawke, so don't expect this to be a sensible and impartial "review". ;)<br/><br/><a href='http://s875.photobucket.com/albums/ab314/Dina67/?action=view&current=GabrielAubry.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380339003i/695865._SX540_.jpg' width='430' height='230' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Hawke alone deserves 5 stars, and I'll just be honest and say that I'd love this book even if the plot was utter crap - which it isn't, of course.<br/><br/>I <s>became obsessed</s> feel in love with Hawke the moment I met him in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/178476.Slave_to_Sensation__Psy_Changeling__1_' title='Slave to Sensation (Psy-Changeling #1) by Nalini Singh' rel='nofollow noopener'>Slave to Sensation</a>, the first book in the series:<br/><i><br/>Hawke was muscular and he was lethal. A predator to the core. His eyes were the same icy blue whet</i></span>
  <span id="freeText10734437748104996394" style="display:none">First off, let me say that I'm completely biased when it comes to Hawke, so don't expect this to be a sensible and impartial "review". ;)<br><br><a href="http://s875.photobucket.com/albums/ab314/Dina67/?action=view&amp;current=GabrielAubry.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380339003i/695865._SX540_.jpg" width="430" height="230" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Hawke alone deserves 5 stars, and I'll just be honest and say that I'd love this book even if the plot was utter crap - which it isn't, of course.<br><br>I <s>became obsessed</s> feel in love with Hawke the moment I met him in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/178476.Slave_to_Sensation__Psy_Changeling__1_" title="Slave to Sensation (Psy-Changeling #1) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Slave to Sensation</a>, the first book in the series:<br><i><br>Hawke was muscular and he was lethal. A predator to the core. His eyes were the same icy blue whether he was in wolf or human form, his hair a thick silver-gold that had nothing to do with age. It echoed his pelt. Of all the changelings Lucas knew, it was Hawke who resembled his beast the most in humanity.<br></i><br><a href="http://s875.photobucket.com/albums/ab314/Dina67/?action=view&amp;current=Psy-Changeling-HawkeMysticWolf.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380339003i/695866._SX540_.jpg" width="430" height="269" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lucas, the hero in that book, was yummylicious on his own way, no question about it, but it was Hawke who grabbed my heart then. I'd been anxiously waiting to read his book ever since, but I knew it would take some time before he was ready...<br><i><br>Sascha took a breath and let her eyes flutter shut. (...) The wolf's emotions struck cold terror into her heart. She'd never felt such pure, unadulterated rage. Dark and violent, it was a scar across his soul. Hawke could function, could rule, but this man would never love, not so long as he was blinded by the red veil of blood and death.<br></i><br>Cold, dangerous, ruthless, tortured... Is it any wonder I fell hard and fast for him? <i>*sighs*</i><br><br>Sienna was introduced in that book too and I immediately sensed she would become a major player in the series, even though she only had a few lines. I didn't see any sexual spark between Hawke and her - thank the gods, because she was only seventeen back then - but it was clear that he let her get away with more than he normally would.<br><br><a href="http://s875.photobucket.com/albums/ab314/Dina67/?action=view&amp;current=SusanCoffey.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380339003i/695867._SX540_.jpg" width="430" height="323" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The tension between them became more evident in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/215643.Visions_of_Heat__Psy_Changeling___2_" title="Visions of Heat (Psy-Changeling, #2) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Visions of Heat</a>, the following book in the series, and I began to wonder what Ms. Singh had in store for them. Hawke's description of Sienna was almost like a declaration of love:<br><i><br>"Sienna's so damn much trouble, I'm starting to think the brat's a she-wolf in bloody disguise."<br></i><br>Aww, comparing her to a she-wolf... High compliment coming from a wolf, don't you think? ;)<br><br>The tension escalated in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/458034.Caressed_By_Ice__Psy_Changeling___3_" title="Caressed By Ice (Psy-Changeling, #3) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Caressed By Ice</a> and I had no more doubts about their pairing.<br><i><br>Sienna could make Hawke lose his cool faster than any other man or woman in the den. (...) Hawke's face darkened. "Keep that damn brat away from me — she's more trouble than a pack of rabid cats."<br></i><br>Yup, it was true love, LOL.<br><br>Naturally, Ms. Singh had to throw another major obstacle in their way...<br><i><br>"Can I ask you something?"<br>Hawke rubbed a hand over Brenna's back. "Go on."<br>"Why haven’t you taken a mate?"<br>(...)<br>Hawke didn't respond for a long time. "She was two years old when we met. I was seven. I knew she was my best friend straight away. As I got older, I also knew she would grow up to become my mate."<br>Brenna didn't want him to continue, a horrible feeling in the pit of her stomach.<br>"She fit me in a way no one else ever will. And she died when she was five and I was ten."<br>A single tear rolled down her face. She wished anything that she could turn back time and save that life, because mating was a one-shot deal. Hawke had found the woman who was meant for him. That didn't happen twice.<br></i><br>No, no, no! What kind of future Hawke and Sienna could have if she was never to be his mate, the one and only woman in the world meant for him? Oh, the pain!<br><br>Ms. Singh, who must be a sadist (I say that with love, LOL), did nothing to soothe my poor nerves in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1830755.Mine_to_Possess__Psy_Changeling___4_" title="Mine to Possess (Psy-Changeling, #4) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Mine to Possess</a>, as neither Hawke nor Sienna made a single appearance in that book. Big bummer!<br><br>Fortunately, Hawke and I didn't have to stay apart for long, as he was back on the scene in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3115070.Hostage_to_Pleasure__Psy_Changeling___5_" title="Hostage to Pleasure (Psy-Changeling, #5) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Hostage to Pleasure</a>. Sienna was still MIA, but one particular dialogue between Lucas and Sacha made me perk up and smile like a ninny:<br><i><br>"That damn wolf. He sent you a present last week."<br>Sascha smiled at the thought of Hawke's flirting. The SnowDancer alpha did it only to jerk Lucas' chain. "I never saw any present. What was it?"<br>"How the hell should I know? I stomped on it and threw it into the deepest crevice I could find." Lucas smirked. "Then I called him to ask how Sienna was doing."<br>She burst out laughing. "Wicked, wicked man." Everyone knew Sienna Lauren was the short fuse on Hawke's temper. The Psy teenager appeared to have made it her mission in life to get on his last nerve. "What did he say?"<br>"That she's planning a party for her eighteenth birthday." The laughter in Lucas's tone told her exactly what Hawke had sounded like as he shared that tidbit.<br></i><br>Woohoo! Sienna was turning eighteen and Hawke wouldn't be able to hold her at arm's length anymore. But what about the darn mating bond they could never share? Oh, the agony!<br><br>As expected, a eighteen-year-old Sienna proved to be dangerous - but not only to Hawke. A Cardinal Psy with undisclosed powerful abilities, her conditioning and shields were crumbling, putting everything and everyone around her in danger.<br><i><br>"I'm the horror in the closet, Sascha, the nightmare even Psy hide from."<br>"Your uncle has extremely powerful abilities — he's learned to control them. So will you."<br>"I’m not like Uncle Judd. I'm worse. You know it and so do I. One slip and boom, I take out the entire den."<br>Sascha held the girl closer, disbelieving. Cardinal Psy with furious combat abilities were beyond deadly. Sienna could possibly take out the SnowDancer den if she lost her grip on her powers. "You've been trying to manage it?"<br>"I shut up everything inside. Everything. I thought if I could hold it, just hold it, it would be fine. But it's not."<br>"Why?" she asked. "Why are you losing control this badly?"<br>The answer, when it came, broke Sascha's heart.<br>"Hawke." It was an almost soundless whisper.<br></i><br>So, another obstacle was thrown on Hawke and Sienna's way... As a Psy with a strong and virulent ability, she couldn't exist without Silence. But she couldn't hold on her conditioning <i>and</i> be around Hawke at the same time either. Darn! Wasn't the impossibility of a mating bond between Hawke and Sienna bad enough? <i>*pouts*</i><br><br>To my dismay, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5628753.Branded_by_Fire__Psy_Changeling___6_" title="Branded by Fire (Psy-Changeling, #6) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Branded by Fire</a> ended with Hawke and Sienna apart. It looked like their story was over, especially after she started hanging around with a gorgeous, loyal, charming DarkRiver cat. Hmmm...<br><br>Once again, the sadist in Ms. Singh kept me on the verge of a breakdown when neither Hawke nor Sienna made an appearance in the following book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6353014.Blaze_of_Memory__Psy_Changeling___7_" title="Blaze of Memory (Psy-Changeling, #7) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Blaze of Memory</a>. They weren't even mentioned! That was cruel! I needed to know if they were really over, if Sienna had found a new lover, and if Hawke was free to be mine. <i>Mine!</i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7044445.Bonds_of_Justice__Psy_Changeling___8_" title="Bonds of Justice (Psy-Changeling, #8) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Bonds of Justice</a> seemed to cement their separation. They were still MIA, but at least they were mentioned:<br><i><br>"Kit would be the better choice for Sienna," Lucas said in a quiet tone that did nothing to hide the depth of his concern for everyone involved. "Hawke isn't going to be easy on any woman he takes as his own. And the fact is, he lost the girl who would've been his mate as a child. I don't know if his wolf will allow him to accept another female on that level."<br></i><br>As much as I wanted Hawke to be mine, I can't say I was happy with that. Despite all the obstacles, I still wanted Hawke and Sienna together, but I began to wonder if Ms. Singh was laying the ground to introduce a plot twist - like, Hawke's mate's unexpected "resurrection"... :-/<br><br>Silly, silly me! <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7831145.Play_of_Passion__Psy_Changeling___9_" title="Play of Passion (Psy-Changeling, #9) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Play of Passion</a> put things back in place again. Hawke and Sienna were definitely meant to be together, yay! The stubborn man was still trying to fight the unwavering pull, but his wolf was tired of waiting and ready to claim what he saw as his:<br><i><br>(...) he surrendered to the wild hunger within and headed out for a run in wolf form.<br>He'd barely cleared the doorway when he caught a scent that instantly ruffled his fur the wrong way. She smelled like autumn fire and some rich, exotic spice. Far too potent a scent for someone so young, someone from whom he should keep his distance. Instead, he drew the spice-laced air into his lungs and ran at a ground-devouring lope that brought him to a small rise from where he could watch his prey.<br>(...)<br>He should step back, should move in the opposite direction.<br>He should.<br>He turned and angled down through the trees until he appeared on the path beside her instead. Jerking back in surprise, Sienna stared at him with wide eyes. When he did nothing but wait for her, she continued on the trail, shooting him small looks filled with suspicion until it became clear he was intent only on keeping her company.<br>Then her stride relaxed, and they walked.<br>In silence.<br></i><br>Sweet!!! Call me crazy, but I can't resist a stalking hero, LOL. And as soon as I finished reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7831145.Play_of_Passion__Psy_Changeling___9_" title="Play of Passion (Psy-Changeling, #9) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Play of Passion</a>, I started counting the days until the release of my beloved Hawke's book. Oh, the anticipation! Four and a half years, that's how long I had to wait for it. What if it didn't fulfill my sky-high expectations? I'd die! (I'm such a drama queen, LOL.)<br><br>Then, to my surprise and utter joy, I was able to get an early copy of this coveted gem, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8712343.Kiss_of_Snow__Psy_Changeling___10_" title="Kiss of Snow (Psy-Changeling, #10) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of Snow</a>. Finally! I'd finally get the answers to the questions that had been plaguing me... Would Hawke be able to claim Sienna as his mate or would they have to settle for a "regular" relationship? ... What would happen when she was no longer able to keep her destructive Psy abilities under control? ... How would the Psy Council's dissolution affect the world? ... Would there be anything left after the Pure Psy unleashed their massive attack on the changeling packs? ... Did the book answer all those questions? Well, you know I <s>can't</s> won't tell you. ;) But I'll let you know this: the series is definitely <i>not</i> over and I can't wait to see what will happen next.<br><br>As with almost all the books in this series, there isn't much I can say here about the continuing story arc that started in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/178476.Slave_to_Sensation__Psy_Changeling__1_" title="Slave to Sensation (Psy-Changeling #1) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Slave to Sensation</a> without giving away spoilers, so I'll keep this short. Unlike some of the previous books, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8712343.Kiss_of_Snow__Psy_Changeling___10_" title="Kiss of Snow (Psy-Changeling, #10) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of Snow</a> showed that the Psy weren't as "weak" as the Changelings (and I) had thought. By "weak", I mean that as much as the Psy had been presented as ruthless and deadly before, I'd never fully felt a real threat to the Changelings. That changed in this book, as it was shown that the Psy <i>could</i> take down the Changelings. Plotwise, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8712343.Kiss_of_Snow__Psy_Changeling___10_" title="Kiss of Snow (Psy-Changeling, #10) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of Snow</a> marks the end of the original story arc of the series. I'm sure all the major players we've met over the years will still be around in the next books, but the series' main focus is likely to change after the latest developments in the Psy-Changeling war.<br><br>Considering Hawke and Sienna's history, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8712343.Kiss_of_Snow__Psy_Changeling___10_" title="Kiss of Snow (Psy-Changeling, #10) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of Snow</a> is filled with sexual tension. They had been dancing around each other for a long time, and it was time to set things right. Hawke, the man and the wolf, had reached the breaking point. He still tried to convince himself to let Sienna go, thinking she deserved better than a man who couldn't give her the mating bond, but the thought of seeing her with another man was enough to drive him insane. He couldn't let her go, not after he claimed skin privileges...<br><i><br>"You want to dance?" Husky words that stroked along her skin like the softest fur.<br>She nodded.<br>"Then we dance." Reaching out, he switched on the vehicle's sound system and input a selection before stepping out.<br>Her door opened as a slow, smoky ballad began to play. "Come."<br>Not sure this wasn't all a dream, she placed her hand in his and, fighting the wild rush of sensation engentlered by his touch and his scent, allowed him to tug her around to the front of the vehicle. "Arms around my neck."<br>The command released her voice. "I thought you weren't being alpha here."<br>"I'm not." Oh.<br>As she raised her arms, she realized her boots gave her enough height to cup his nape with one hand, while she placed the other on the muscled warmth of his shoulder. When he shifted position so that his jaw rubbed against her temple, her heart began to thud fast as a jackhammer.<br>Teeth nipped at her ear.<br>She jumped.<br>"Pay attention." A rumbling growl.<br>(...)<br>"Sienna." A deep murmur against her skin, his lips brushing her temple. "This can't be. You know that."<br>"No," she said. "Not tonight." She wanted to dance with him, be a woman in the arms of a man who made every part of her awaken in a hunger she'd never expected to feel and who, for this magical moment, was hers.<br>His jaw, heavy with stubble, rubbed against her temple again as he shifted his hold to press her closer. Then, as the music played, as the night grew softer and quieter, they danced.<br></i><br><a href="http://s875.photobucket.com/albums/ab314/Dina67/?action=view&amp;current=Danceunderthemoonlight.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380339003i/695868._SX540_.jpg" width="430" height="322" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh Hawke, you romantic beast! Call me "baby", chase me, bite me, mark me... You've ruined me for other men!<br><br>As for Sienna, her maturity came as no surprise to me. She was "only" nineteen, but she was no teenager. Sure, she had a couple of hissy fits that could be labeled teen-ish, but she was mostly old beyond her years, due to the life she'd had before her defection from the PsyNet. So the age issue - Hawke was thirty-four - was never a problem to me. She was strong, level-headed, unafraid to go after what she wanted - and willing to cut loose if that was proven to be out of her reach. She was done hanging around Hawke and waiting for him, so he either claimed her or stopped acting possessive about her. Good for her! If only she had more time before her deadly Psy ability took over...<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Sienna unleashed:<br><br><a href="http://s875.photobucket.com/albums/ab314/Dina67/?action=view&amp;current=FireWoman.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380339003i/695869.jpg" width="430" height="304" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Now, I have to say that I could have done with a little less sexual tension. Hawke and Sienna were on the verge of going for the ultimate skin privilege only to be interrupted <i>so many freaking times</i>, I was pulling my hair in frustation when they finally managed to go through with it. Halfway through the book, I began to worry about his health. Thankfully, dying from blue balls is only a myth, or he'd have perished on the spot. ;)<br><br>Besides the two main storylines (Hawke and Sienna's relationship and the Psy-Changeling war), there was also a surprising (to me) and sweet secondary romance <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[between Walker, Sienna's uncle, and Lara, the SnowDancer healer, <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> that made reading this book even more enjoyable. I liked both of them and was very happy to see them together.<br><br>And for those die-hard fans like me, who have been following this series since the beginning, you'll be glad to know that all the heroes and heroines from the previous books had their share in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8712343.Kiss_of_Snow__Psy_Changeling___10_" title="Kiss of Snow (Psy-Changeling, #10) by Nalini Singh" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of Snow</a>. A few of them were only mentioned, but most shared some scenes with Hawke and/or Sienna. Lucas and Sascha's participation was special and I was thrilled for them. And for those who love Judd, well, get ready for a smoking hot scene with the Man of Ice. Yowza!<br><br>Last but not least, let me tell you how much I loved the final scene in the book:<br><i><br>"What's your full name?"<br>Hawke's wolf flashed in his eyes, the ice blue glittering with the same amusement that had his cheeks creasing. "What brought that on?"<br>"I refuse to be in the dark. Tell."<br>Leaning down, he nipped at her jaw, a quick, affectionate bite that had her jerking. "No distracting me, I want to know."<br>Another small bite before he whispered it in her ear.<br>She blinked.<br>"No."<br>He growled, but it was playful. "Don't you like it?"<br>"It's beautiful, you know it is." Perfect for him.<br>(...)<br>"What about me?" she asked. "Do I take your last name?"<br>"Do you want to?" A tilt of his head, the wolf watchful but not demanding.<br>She considered the question with care, thinking of who she'd been, who she was now.<br>"Yes," she said at last, "but I'd like to keep mine, too. It's a part of me."<br>Lips against her own, a wolf's kiss. "That works fine for me... Sienna Lauren <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Snow <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>."<br></i><br>I think I'll have to change my last name too. Dina <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Snow <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Yeah, I like the sound of that. ;)<br><br>Considering how much I had anticipated this book and how high my expectations were, I'm glad to say I was more than satisfied with it. Ha, what an understatement! I loved it! Loved. It! It wasn't perfect and I thought Ms. Singh could have handled a couple of things differently, but that didn't dampen the enjoyment of this read.<br><br><b>Final verdict:</b> It's a keeper!<br><br><i>Note: As I was writing this, I was aware that it was nothing like a review should be. It was just my gushing, incoherent and deranged collection of thoughts on Hawke, my favorite shifter ever. What can I say? I had to pay hommage to him and I hope I did him justice.</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer390501594" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18353657165886249149"><b><br/>I started my re-read and have only one thing in my mind for this:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383785ra/742131.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/>This book just blew my mind <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=explosionta5.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380387456ra/747477.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/>Bye Bye brain <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=67639-1.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/367658.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a> <br/><br/>After waiting through 9 books to get to this one </b>(yes, freaking 9 <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=998987.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/347827.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a>, freaking (although fantastic) books)<b> I have to say - IT DIDN'T DISSAPOINT! <br/><br/>Kiss of Snow is one of the best books I've read <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=279453.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/360663.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a> (not just this year :P ) it deserves atleast a 100 of these guys <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=279453.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/360663.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a> </b><br/><br/><br/><br/>After dancing around each other for the last nine books (nine!!), Hawke has reached the limits of his self-restraint, and Sienna's</span>
  <span id="freeText18353657165886249149" style="display:none"><b><br>I started my re-read and have only one thing in my mind for this:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383785ra/742131.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>This book just blew my mind <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=explosionta5.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380387456ra/747477.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Bye Bye brain <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=67639-1.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/367658.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <br><br>After waiting through 9 books to get to this one </b>(yes, freaking 9 <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=998987.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/347827.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>, freaking (although fantastic) books)<b> I have to say - IT DIDN'T DISSAPOINT! <br><br>Kiss of Snow is one of the best books I've read <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=279453.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/360663.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> (not just this year :P ) it deserves atleast a 100 of these guys <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=279453.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/360663.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> </b><br><br><br><br>After dancing around each other for the last nine books (nine!!), Hawke has reached the limits of his self-restraint, and Sienna's control over her abilities is virtually non-existent when she's around him. She's no longer a teenager defected from the Psy, she's a member of the wolf pack and trained as a soldier. What few know, is that she's the most powerful Psy that ever existed. A X-Psy, rarity in itself, she's a cardinal, with powers beyond measure. Hawke is the wolf pack's alpha. And when I say alpha, you can imagine the most alpha male you've ever read and multiply with a 100 <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=1059282649.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380372925ra/726346.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> He is intense, his inner wolf is almost always at the surface, wild, posessive and sexy as freaking hell! <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=830689743.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/357707.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> The chemistry between them was bursting all over, and when he finally decided to go for it (finally, finally), oh boy, that caused my total meltdown <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=767622.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222758i/362324.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><br><br>They are both strong personalities, Hawke, of course, being alpha, and Sienna, being trained as a child to be the perfect killing machine. They fight all the time <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=2783945661.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/361318.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> and flirt all the time <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=706146.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/388551.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> and the sex scenes <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=fansmiley.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/357930.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> HOT! Amazingly HOT!<br><br><br><br>Those two aside, I loved all the other litte stories in here, Sascha had her baby, Walker and Lara had a lovely romance, we get to see almost every couple from the previous books, Judd having a slightly bigger role here (did I mention I just love him &lt;3 ), and The Ghost helped him with Sienna!!! Who the hell is that guy??? <br><br><br><br>So, this was such a great book, from page one I was like this <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=311685.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/359489.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>, mixed with stupid sensless giggling and grinning and clutching my e-reader and basically acting like a crazed teenager hahahahah I guess the anticipation got to me <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=703126.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/363966.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><b>Some of my favorite scenes:</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[...- Sienna asking Hawke not to touch her<br>- when Hawke went to the bar to pick them up, oh how he went wild <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=938748.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374123ra/728036.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>- Hawke and Sienna dancing by the car <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=836920.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/356484.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> I think this one's my favorite, just beautiful<br>- their "play" in the forest, when she set traps for him <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=703126.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/363966.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>- the second time Hawke went to the bar <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=355146.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/362691.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> oh I couldn't stop laughing at that one XD<br>- the strip-poker <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=1700353446.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/362994.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>- the sex in the cabin <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=830689743.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/357707.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> one of the best sex scenes I've ever read! Just wow!<br>- when he finds her in the forest after she <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[runs away <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>- the ending, in the battle, when Hawke stopped her <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=468813.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/374889.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>A fabulous book, I really don't know if anything will top it, this was just perfect! I'm looking forward to #11, I heard there was going to be more Hawke and Sienna in that one, and the plots revolving around packs - I simply love them <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=bliss.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/357951.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2209729060" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7274135477482506330"><b>4.5 a little confused Stars</b><br/><br/><br/><a href='https://imgur.com/8ewjy7f' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1513324656ra/24681347.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>************Spoilers***************************</b><br/><br/>I have been looking forward to Hawke and Sienna book since book one. Annnnd I was not disappointed. I knew going into this book that Hawke's "mate" died when they were children and so he is not suppose to be able to mate again. As wolves only get one mate. So my only problem with this book was the confusion over Hawke and Sienna's mating. I was prepared for Hawke to just love her or for him to figure out that Rissa was</span>
  <span id="freeText7274135477482506330" style="display:none"><b>4.5 a little confused Stars</b><br><br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/8ewjy7f" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1513324656ra/24681347.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>************Spoilers***************************</b><br><br>I have been looking forward to Hawke and Sienna book since book one. Annnnd I was not disappointed. I knew going into this book that Hawke's "mate" died when they were children and so he is not suppose to be able to mate again. As wolves only get one mate. So my only problem with this book was the confusion over Hawke and Sienna's mating. I was prepared for Hawke to just love her or for him to figure out that Rissa wasn't really his mate. I was looking forward to finding out which scenario it was going to be, but instead Nalini Singh's just kinda glossed over it. Sienna and Hawke did mate, but he still talked about Rissa like she was his mate so wtf? Was Rissa his mate and because she was too young and they didn't claim each other he got a do over?? Did I miss something as I was listening to the audiobook?(that could totally be the case as I had a house full of kids and I had to keep pulling my earbuds out to yell stop picking your nose, or kicking your sister, or breathing your brother's air lol) I totally felt Hawke and Sienna's love for each other, but the unanswered question about the whole mating and the following confusing left me feeling annoyed. Overall I still loved this book. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7274135477482506330" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer149132488" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2956456581441188958">6-1-11~I'm replacing my old review with this one, as promised, b/c this one contains spoilers for the book.<br/><br/>A little background…I picked up Nalini Singh’s Psy-Changling series on a whim back in 2006 with Slave to Sensation…and when I was finished with that book, I was immediately drawn to Hawke’s story and my fervent hope that eventually A) it’d get written soon and B) his HEA was Sienna Lauren who was 16 at the time. Each subsequent book after that I read hoping for bits and pieces of Hawke’s st</span>
  <span id="freeText2956456581441188958" style="display:none">6-1-11~I'm replacing my old review with this one, as promised, b/c this one contains spoilers for the book.<br /><br />A little background…I picked up Nalini Singh’s Psy-Changling series on a whim back in 2006 with Slave to Sensation…and when I was finished with that book, I was immediately drawn to Hawke’s story and my fervent hope that eventually A) it’d get written soon and B) his HEA was Sienna Lauren who was 16 at the time. Each subsequent book after that I read hoping for bits and pieces of Hawke’s story and wanting to know what Sienna was up to. Suffice it to say, this was my most anticipated read of like, forever.<br /><br />Cut to 2011.<br /><br />Ms. Singh was kind enough to send me an ARC (which I found out I would be getting during my birthday week—which was the best birthday present of ever) and I literally devoured this book when it came in the mail.<br /><br />Kiss of Snow is amazing. It’s amazing, intriguing, and delicious. There’s a lot that goes on in this book, and so many storylines are finished and begun that I can see why Ms. Singh said that it was going to be longer than her others in this series. It will be on my re-read shelf forever. I’ve re-read it about 20 times already…and it never gets old. NEVER.<br /><br />Hawke is the alpha of the SnowDancer wolf pack…a position he’s held since he was 15 when all of the adults in the pack were betrayed by a trusted member of the pack and subsequently destroyed from within. It’s something that has haunted the pack ever since, and is one of the reasons why Hawke is so protective of not only the pack hierarchy but in maintaining pack honor and loyalty. He loves his pack with a ferocity that is almost overwhelming in nature…he’d do anything for them…and they’d do anything for him.<br /><br />He also lost the girl that would have been his mate when he was 10. It’s unusual for anyone to discover their mate that early (he was 7 at the time) and he lost her 3 years later. It devastated him as a child and he’s convinced himself that he’ll never mate. Ever.<br /><br />Imagine his surprise when he realizes that he’s inexorably drawn to one Sienna Lauren, a Psy defector who entered his pack with her family 3 years ago. He’s tried to keep her at a distance…and so far it’s worked. Until now.<br /><br />Sienna is an X-Psy…the only one that she knows of in existence. Not only that…she’s a cardinal X-Psy…something that, as far as she knows, has never existed before. She considers SnowDancer her extended family, and is as ferociously protective of them as she is of her immediate family. Her attraction to Hawke threatens to overwhelm the shields that she desperately needs to contain her abilities. That doesn’t mean, however, that she doesn’t push his buttons, push him, whenever the mood strikes her, trying to get him to see her as she so fervently wants him to.<br /><br />What she hadn’t realized until now…he does see her. He always has. That’s been the problem.<br /><br />The dance between the two takes up two thirds of the book. The attraction between them is palpable and obvious…but the conflict comes from them actually having to learn to understand each other, and learn each other so that they can become the true alpha pair that SnowDancer needs.<br /><br />Nalini always writes awesome alpha male characters, and Hawke is the alpha of all alphas in this book. He’s a force to be reckoned with. He’s confident in his position as alpha, in his physical abilities and in his physical attractiveness. He loves his pack, and would do anything for them…while at the same time, he’s demanding of those around him, and uses his dominance to ruthless effect. It is this very dominance that is the main reason why, as mentioned early on in the book, any female would have to have brass balls to take him on.<br /><br />Sienna Lauren has them…and more. She’s had to live with and learn to control her formidable abilities since she was very young, a discipline that has affected her profoundly…and yet she has still been able to keep the core of who she is true. She’s fiercely loyal to those that she considers her own, and her love for her immediate family, and the SnowDancer wolf pack (whom she considers an extended family) is palpable, and a driving force behind a lot of her actions concerning her abilities. She’s funny and quick, and while she may be young, the things that she’s had to go through in her life has shaped the woman she’s become, and she’s stronger for it. A strength she needs when she finally decides to pit the force of her personality against that of Hawke’s. Reading how well the two of them compliment each other, in both public and private scenarios, is a joy.<br /><br />One of the main conflicts between Sienna and Hawke, aside from the age issue (which was handled really well early in the book) is Sienna’s desire for the mating bond, and Hawke’s belief in his inability to give it to her. How this conflict was wrapped up was extremely satisfying for me, since it had been an ongoing debate between a friend and I for the past year. <br /><br />What was even more fun to read about is Hawke teaching Sienna to play. Aside from the huge sexual attraction between them…Sienna has never played before, since at an early age, the destructiveness of her abilities has been drilled into her…and she’s never been able to be anything but an adult. The parts where Hawke and Sienna are just hanging out and enjoying each other’s company are some of the best parts of the book, especially since there is a war that is about to explode between the two strongest changeling packs, SnowDancer and DarkRiver, and the Pure Psy zealots under Henry Scott. With SnowDancer being the largest of the two changeling packs, that’s where most of the strategic strikes against changelings occur. And boy are the strikes devastating. The war is most definitely on. It is not tied up as completely as I would have liked, or even expected, but it is finished in a way that completes the arc while also allowing for other stories in this universe to continue.<br /><br />There are some really great moments in the book too, that have nothing to do with Hawke and Sienna, and everything to do with the love of the pack for their alpha. They understand the sacrifices that he’s had to make to be the leader that they need, and they’re grateful and love him for it. I don’t often verbally “Aww!” while reading books, but there is a scene later in the book between the pack and their alpha that definitely made me verbally “Aww!”.<br /><br />Both Judd and Brenna make significant appearances in this book, and Judd’s just as awesome as usual. He’s still one of my most favorite heroes in the Psy/Changeling universe outside of Hawke, and he had some really great moments with both Hawke and Sienna. The poignant moments that he had with his mate, Brenna, were great, and really spoke to the depth of love those two share. Lucas and Sascha are also in the book quite a bit, with both of them helping both Hawke and Sienna learn to understand each other, fight against the Psy and Henry Scott...and most importantly...the baby is finally born!<br /><br />We also get to see more of Kit, whom I’d been pretty indifferent to in past books. Seeing him through Sienna’s eyes makes me interested in his story. There’s also quite a bit with Walker and Lara (who get an emotional side romance as well), Nikita and Kaleb, the Ghost, Vaughn, Riley, Indigo and Andrew. I would have loved to see more Vasic…but you can’t have everything…and there is plenty in this book that made up for it. The Arrow Squad has always intrigued me, and where they end up falling in this war on Silence still remains to be seen.<br /><br /><br />We even get a flashback scene to that very first meeting between Hawke and Sienna! I LOVED THAT. Seriously…I had been wanting something like that for years…right along with a hint at the shenanigans that happened around Sienna’s 18th birthday party…and we got that too! This book hit every note that I could possibly want it to hit…and a few more.<br /><br />Overall, the love story between Hawke and Sienna is an emotional one, and by the time they both come out on the other side, they truly are the alpha pair that I envisioned all those years ago when I read StS, and I noticed Sienna noticing Hawke…and Hawke noticing back.<br /><br />To sum up this book in 2 words…Awesome Sauce. This book is awesome sauce. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2956456581441188958" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText9016887396281064739" style="display:none"><b>Hawke Snow (SnowDancer Alpha) and Sienna Lauren (Psy)</b><br /><br /><i>“Except I never had a prayer when it came to you. You’re in my every breath and every thought, intertwined so deep inside me that love’s not a strong enough word—you have my devotion, your name branded on my soul, <b>my wolf yours to command</b>. A hundred years? It’ll never be enough. Their story was building since several books until now. In the previous books Hawke was always trying to avoid Sienna and Sienna always seemed to want something from Hawke.<br /><br />Their book starts in the same manner. Sienna now is an adult who is playful and happy, she likes having a good time, she has good friends and she is more balanced with her powers. Moreover she likes teasing Hawke secretly hoping that at some point he will “break".<br />Hawke tries to resist by running away all the time and by punishing Sienna all the time for little things, while he has vowed to stay faithful to the ghost of his intended mate. He never succeeds to get her Sienna of his head. The funny thing is that everyone has realised his feelings. Some even tease him without taking into account that he is a scary Alpha wolf.<br /><br />I loved the fact that Hawke and Sienna dance and play around each other. It is like they have started a mating dance without realising it.<br /><br />The problems that they need to face are two (except the memory of a dead girl of course):<br />1.	Enemies who want to destroy the Snowdancer pack and who keep attacking <br />2.	The finite of Sienna’s life. <span id="freeTextContainer11803279924063954130">Update - and it's as good the x-time as it was the first time after another reread, I'm happy to say I just love Hawke and Sienna. <br/><br/>✵ ✦ ✷ ✫ ✷ ✦ ✧ ✵ ✧ ✵ ✦ ✷ ✫ ✷ ✦ ✧ ✵ ✧ ✵ ✦ ✷ ✫ ✷ ✦ ✧ ✵ ✧ ✵ <br/><br/><br/>This is HANDS DOWNS the BEST BOOK in the Psy Changeling series.<br/><br/>It deserves 6 stars!!!<br/><br/>Kiss of Snow was everything I hoped for and so much more. <br/><br/>Finally, finally, after nine books of waiting, Hawke and Sienna finally had their HEA. <br/><br/>Nalini Singh had us waiting for a long time and it worked. The anticipation almost </span>
  <span id="freeText11803279924063954130" style="display:none">Update - and it's as good the x-time as it was the first time after another reread, I'm happy to say I just love Hawke and Sienna. <br /><br />✵ ✦ ✷ ✫ ✷ ✦ ✧ ✵ ✧ ✵ ✦ ✷ ✫ ✷ ✦ ✧ ✵ ✧ ✵ ✦ ✷ ✫ ✷ ✦ ✧ ✵ ✧ ✵ <br /><br /><br />This is HANDS DOWNS the BEST BOOK in the Psy Changeling series.<br /><br />It deserves 6 stars!!!<br /><br />Kiss of Snow was everything I hoped for and so much more. <br /><br />Finally, finally, after nine books of waiting, Hawke and Sienna finally had their HEA. <br /><br />Nalini Singh had us waiting for a long time and it worked. The anticipation almost killed me. But the delivery just amazed me.<br /><br />After many teasers, tidbits and rumors, Hawke finally wrestled his demons, misgivings and listened to his wolf and went after what he really wanted - Sienna. As the pack alpha, such a decision was not easy, and his struggles were evident and raw. The age gap was a huge consideration on his side, a hurdle that felt as deep as a chasm. His concern was understandable but Sienna, so mature for her age, kicked that notion to the curb pretty quickly. And I just wanted to stand up and applaud her!!!<br /><br />That girl was something else!! Sienna was strong, down-to-earth, knew exactly what she wanted, and was prepared for the outcome as well for whatever the future held and threw into her path. She would conquer it all!<br /><br />The sexual tension was literally explosive. The wait for Hawke and Sienna's HEA was as excruciating as rewarding. Both needed time to accept the fact that they were missing pieces to each other's happiness. They completed one another. With Sienna, Hawke could just be Hawke, and in contrast Sienna didn't have to be afraid letting go. <br /><br />They complimented each other in the best of ways. And filled the missing pieces to their happiness.<br /><br />Kiss of Snow is the best book she's every written and as a bonus, Hawke and Sienna's story continues in Tangle of Need. One and a half books of Hawke and Sienna - how PERFECT is that!!!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11803279924063954130" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_150084753" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/150084753" />
    <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner"><img alt="Mandi Schreiner" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368979996p2/2704703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/150084753?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mandi Schreiner" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner">Mandi Schreiner</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2704703-mandi-schreiner?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2704703-mandi-schreiner?shelf=favorite-2011">favorite-2011</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer150084753" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8015130226169878302">Favorite Quote: “You sure you want to play with the wolf, baby?”<br/><br/>Favorite Quote #2: The crowd was chanting, “kiss, kiss, kiss” when Hawke walked inside.<br/><br/>That was when Sienna learned the meaning of the term alpha.<br/><br/>Favorite Quote #3: "Scared?" Hawke’s smile held no humor. "You should be baby." Then he kissed her and it was no tender exploration, no playful tease. This was the kiss of a man who knew precisely what he wanted.<br/><br/>Hawke, alpha of the SnowDancer pack and Sienna, a Psy that has found refuge wi</span>
  <span id="freeText8015130226169878302" style="display:none">Favorite Quote: “You sure you want to play with the wolf, baby?”<br /><br />Favorite Quote #2: The crowd was chanting, “kiss, kiss, kiss” when Hawke walked inside.<br /><br />That was when Sienna learned the meaning of the term alpha.<br /><br />Favorite Quote #3: "Scared?" Hawke’s smile held no humor. "You should be baby." Then he kissed her and it was no tender exploration, no playful tease. This was the kiss of a man who knew precisely what he wanted.<br /><br />Hawke, alpha of the SnowDancer pack and Sienna, a Psy that has found refuge with the SnowDancers have been dancing around each other for some time now. They both might have acted on their lust for each other but Sienna is just now 19. Sienna is also an extremely powerful X Psy – if her powers get out of control, she can decimate everything around her. Now living outside of Silence, no one knows exactly what is going to happen to her. Her powers are extremely volatile. She may be the only X cardinal ever born. No X-Psy has lives past their 25th birthday. And that was within Silence.<br /><br />Hawke can’t deny the attraction, but he lost his mate when he was very young. Knowing a wolf only mates once, he doesn’t know if Sienna can handle the demands his wolf would place upon her. But as he says – Pack is life, and Pack knows these two are meant for each other. With their support (and threats from Sienna’s uncle) these two take a chance.<br /><br />Meanwhile, the Psy Council is disintegrating. Sides are being taken, betrayals are in progress. There are those who want a race of Pure Psy – where Silence is law. While a civil war is on the horizon and some want to take the shifters down with them.<br /><br />Kiss of Snow is one of my most highly anticipated books of 2011. I fell in love with Hawke many books ago, and we finally get his story with Sienna. First let me say I love how Nalini writes her shifters. So sexy, sensual and physical. And Hawke does not disappoint. Some of the things that come out of his mouth melted me into a puddle of goo. He calls Sienna “baby” a lot and it’s hot. He has to learn to walk the line between being Sienna’s alpha and her lover. He is of course alpha down to his core, and Sienna soon learns playing with his wolf is more fun than she ever thought. They play games, they dance around one another and in the end, they have a beautiful relationship.<br /><br />While the sexual tension is off the wall, halfway through the book, maybe even a little farther I was ready for it to progress to more than just tension. There are so many “almost” moments – they almost kiss, they almost embrace, they almost get physical. But Hawke’s phone rings, or Psy attack, or someone interrupts them. At a certain point it became a little frustrating and distracting. But by the end of the book I was able to look back on their moments together with fondness.<br /><br />Sienna is a X-Psy, and kind of in the dark with how to control her powers and what her eventual outcome will be. At a young age, she was taken from her home to be Ming’s protégé. She went into silence by the age of nine. There is a lot of unknown for her out in the “real world.” There is rumor of an elusive journal written in the 70’s that might give her some answers, and this plays in well in the book. I think Nalini Singh does a nice job portraying Sienna – she has inner strength and confidence, but when her power flares up she really loses all control.<br /><br />I have been disappointed in the past few books with how the Psy war has progressed – or how it has not progressed. In Kiss of Snow I think that storyline has a little more meat. I still want more – maybe just more from the Psy’s point of view. But at least in this one, the Psy mean business and it felt more like they are a threat to the shifters.<br /><br />Walker Lauren, Sienna’s uncle has a really nice romance in this one with Lara, the SnowDancer healer. I really liked both of them and thought their romance brought a lot to this story. We also get a lot with Judd, Sienna’s other uncle since he is so close with Sienna and helps her with her volatile powers. Oh Judd – you sexy former Psy. He has some great lines and one in particular very smexy scene. It’s so nice we get an intimate glimpse into some of the characters that have already had their book.<br /><br />Sascha and Lucas have a storyline that will make you smile. I really enjoy the relationship the Cats now have with the wolves. It feels like a brotherly relationship with good natured bickering – very entertaining to read.<br /><br />For such an anticipated book, Kiss of Snow delivers. I even think this one can be read as a stand alone. You might be a bit confused on the Psy war, but overall I think it would read well on it’s own. Of course, this entire series is great, and I recommend it to everyone.<br /><br />Rating: B+</span>
  <a data-text-id="8015130226169878302" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9758258263877994933">5+ stars – Paranormal Romance<br/><br/>WOWZA! The most anticipated installment in the phenomenal <i>Psy-Changeling</i> series definitely delivers the goods and lives up to the hype. It’s an intense, passionate, and emotional epic romance with smoldering sensuality and thrilling action that is pure tribute to Hawke fanatics. It satisfied my super high expectations and then some. I was completely and utterly captivated by every word from beginning to end, and my only complaint is that I didn’t want it to be over. </span>
  <span id="freeText9758258263877994933" style="display:none">5+ stars – Paranormal Romance<br><br>WOWZA! The most anticipated installment in the phenomenal <i>Psy-Changeling</i> series definitely delivers the goods and lives up to the hype. It’s an intense, passionate, and emotional epic romance with smoldering sensuality and thrilling action that is pure tribute to Hawke fanatics. It satisfied my super high expectations and then some. I was completely and utterly captivated by every word from beginning to end, and my only complaint is that I didn’t want it to be over. I loved it, loved it, <i>loved</i> it! <br><br>Hawke in all his alpha, growly glory is a sexy, magnificent thing to behold. I want to take a big bite out of him, and have him bite me (all over!) in return. YUM! Don’t get me wrong...I love Hawke and Sienna together and think they’re an amazing, unforgettable Romancelandia couple. But I still want to be Hawke’s mate and have his wolf babies. <i>*sighs and swoons*</i> Oh wait, I’m already mated to Lucas. I guess I’ll have to <s>beg</s> settle for being the center of a wolf/panther sandwich. <i>*naughty girl grin*</i> <br><br><b>H</b>ot<br><b>A</b>lpha<br><b>W</b>olf<br><b>K</b>iss me for<br><b>E</b>ternity!!!!<br><br>My favorite quotes:<br><br><i>She came to, to find a very satisfied wolf at her side. He was drawing patterns on the sweat-sheened skin of her navel with his finger. “How was dessert?” she asked, her throat a husky reminder that she’d screamed at the end. A flash of teeth. “I plan to go back for seconds in a bit.” She sucked in a breath. “Bad wolf.” Sliding down his hand, he tugged at her damp curls. “Hungry wolf.” Right then, Sienna knew she was sunk. Absolutely and gloriously.</i><br><br><i>“You’re in my every breath and every thought, intertwined so deep inside me that love’s not a strong enough word—you have my devotion, your name branded on my soul, my wolf yours to command. A hundred years? It’ll never be enough. I want eternity.”</i><br><br><i>“You have the power to tear me to pieces, to wound me so deep and true that I’ll never recover.”</i><br><br>Hawke in his majestically beautiful wolf form (note the “Kiss of Snow” on his nose):<br><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=16qk5u.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1124738912" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1124738912" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1124738912?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101528723" href="/book/show/10863950-kiss-of-snow">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=authors-p-z">authors-p-z</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=lendable">lendable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=favorites-books">favorites-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=vampire-shapeshifters">vampire-shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1124738912" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14647019147884180145">Kiss of Snow is book #10 in Nalini Singh’s stunning the Psy-Changeling Series. I have been waiting for a very long time for Hawke’s story, every since he was introduced in Slave to Sensation, the 1st book in the Series. Somehow I had always hoped that he would get together with Sienna Lauren…..and yes, after 9 books, I finally got my wish.<blockquote>
  
    <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444656276ra/16532424.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_n2l5oxDHk81ttn473o1_250_zpsf4hlf9ve.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  
</blockquote>This is their story. And what a beautiful one it was. Kiss of Snow is one of my favorite books in this series and there’s only one word I can descr</span>
  <span id="freeText14647019147884180145" style="display:none">Kiss of Snow is book #10 in Nalini Singh’s stunning the Psy-Changeling Series. I have been waiting for a very long time for Hawke’s story, every since he was introduced in Slave to Sensation, the 1st book in the Series. Somehow I had always hoped that he would get together with Sienna Lauren…..and yes, after 9 books, I finally got my wish.<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444656276ra/16532424.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_n2l5oxDHk81ttn473o1_250_zpsf4hlf9ve.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>This is their story. And what a beautiful one it was. Kiss of Snow is one of my favorite books in this series and there’s only one word I can describe what Hawke and Sienna’s path to finding their HEA…………<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444656276ra/16532425.gif" alt=" photo Fantastic_zpshdmoqj6y.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote><b>What made this book and this story so special for me:</b><br><br><b>Hawke:</b> I fell in love with this character from the very first time we were introduced. Pure alpha male, sexy and passionate who takes his responsibilities as leader of the SnowDancer pack seriously. How he fights the attraction and feelings for Sienna, using every reason imaginable why he should not even think that him and Sienna together is a good thing for her. <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444656276i/16532426.jpg" alt=" photo images_zpsda462393.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote><b>Sienna:</b> We have seen her developing from a teenager, when she and her family arrived at the SnowDance world. She’s had to grow fast and being a strong Psy, and at the age of nineteen, is stronger, independent, mature than most women of her age. There was so much more to her beneath that delicate and young person. She has always had feeling for Hawke and is totally sure that she’s meant to be with him. I loved her maturity and how she fought for Hawke. Wanting him to see the person she now was……how she dealt with his stubbornness when it came to her….<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444656276i/16532427.jpg" alt=" photo 3cef33cbffca214456840eee506a38e4_zpsgkinvyqw.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote><br><br><b>The development of Hawke and Sienna’s relationship:</b> The two have been dancing around each other since they first met, with Hawke fighting his feeling for her and the obstacles he believes stand in their way to being together. Their journey together is so emotional and so beautiful to watch as they overcome the obstacles in their path to being together.<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444656276i/16532426.jpg" alt=" photo images_zpsda462393.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>The depth of Hawke’s feelings for Sienna are absolutely touching. And seeing him opening up to her and admitting how deep and everlasting his love is for her is so damn beautiful……<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444656276i/16532428.jpg" alt=" photo eyes20lips20face-3_zpscqfyuqbn.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>Their chemistry, their banter and watching them finally giving in to their feelings was an emotional and incredible moment. The gentleness, care and softness Hawke showed Sienna when they first make love made it one of the most sensual and beautiful scenes ever.<br><br>Another thing I so enjoyed was seeing the playful side of Hawke……okay, I had seen that playfulness in the previous books, but in this book…..took it to another level. Sweet …Adorable …..Irresistible……Sexy…..<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444656276i/16532431.jpg" alt=" photo aa89e2740281aaad6f06026404a39774201_zpspdqjp4gn.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote><br><b>The world building:</b> The continuation of the battle for power and scheming between the Psy Council makes me wonder where it’s going to lead to next. Loved learning more about the DarkRiver pack and their world.<br><br><b>Loved characters:</b> Love how the author weaves the lives of the characters we have come to life into each book.<br><br>Loved seeing the continuation and new surprises in Lucas and Sasha’s lives.<br><br>So excited to have been able to get a bit on Walker Lauren and SnowDancer’s healer, Lara and can’t wait for their <br><br>Arrow Aden – I am so looking forward to getting to know more about this character.<br><br>Kiss of Snow is one of the favorite books in this series. It was more exciting and fantastic than what I had hoped for. Romance, everlasting love, wonderful characters, fast paced, twists and turns and more.<br><br>This is one series I can more than recommend to every PNR lovers and even if you have never read paranormal romance….try this one. You will not be disappointed.<br><br><b>My favorite quote:</b><br><blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444656443i/16532455.jpg" alt=" photo 159f1185ddac3d73b0bb58fe4b1a80d9_zpsb3219508.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="14647019147884180145" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2384301311416676430">2.5<br/>Unpopular opinion here!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1477600588ra/20970534.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I've been waiting to read this one for a long time now! And what I found is well... rather disappointing. <br/>I was expecting a lot from Hawk. Or well, a lot more than this. Sienna wasn't too bad, but I still wanted more from her. <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474483655ra/20606364.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I really didn't feel any chemistry between them and their story was of no particular interest. I was more excited about the background plot than about their love thingie. It's the only reason I gave this story 2.5 stars (3 GR ones), because the ov</span>
  <span id="freeText2384301311416676430" style="display:none">2.5<br>Unpopular opinion here!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1477600588ra/20970534.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've been waiting to read this one for a long time now! And what I found is well... rather disappointing. <br>I was expecting a lot from Hawk. Or well, a lot more than this. Sienna wasn't too bad, but I still wanted more from her. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474483655ra/20606364.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really didn't feel any chemistry between them and their story was of no particular interest. I was more excited about the background plot than about their love thingie. It's the only reason I gave this story 2.5 stars (3 GR ones), because the overall plot was damn exciting! <br><br>Maybe I had too high expectations, but it's all Singh's fault! If this series had sucked, then my expectations would have been lower. But I really really wanted Hawk's story! And then I get this...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386675631ra/7418668.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Even more, their age difference was a bit strange to me. Ok, not the age difference, but the way he treats her. It just feels weird... From all these stories, he is like 40ish and she's 19. And a virgin. And yeah, she had the troubling past and she was more mature and blah blah blah, but she's a 19-year-old virgin. She should have been treated a bit differently.<br><br><br>Ah well, at least the plot was fun. And it did make me a bit curious to see what's next, so all in all, it was still a good book. Not a great one, but good nonetheless. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1476056527ra/20796754.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

</b><br><br>Oh...I also get lady boners for strong heroines. Did I mention all that Power Sienna wields?!! Damn!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1599915477ra/30096917.gif" width="400" height="152" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
